The National Government Bans the Manufacture of Morphine in Sichuan Province

Orders Liu Xiang to Investigate and Punish

The National Government yesterday specially ordered Liu Xiang, the commander of the 21st Army, to investigate and ban the morphine manufacturing plants in Chongqing, Wanxian, and Fuzhou. The order stated, "According to the Executive Yuan's report, the Hubei Provincial Government reported that Zhao Tiegong, the magistrate of Yichang County and chairman of the municipal council, reported that the harm of morphine is extremely pervasive, and earnestly requests a strict ban to save the people's lives and strengthen the race. It is true that opium is more harmful than floods and beasts, and morphine is the essence of opium juice, and its harm is even more than opium ten thousand times over. If a person becomes addicted to this vice, they will become chronically ill and unable to recover within three years. It has been found that in recent years, large factories have been opened in Chongqing, Wanxian, and Fuzhou, collecting opium from all over Sichuan and neighboring provinces to extract the essence to make morphine. It is light, convenient, and easy to transport and sell. As the border areas connect to Sichuan, they are transportation hubs, leading to an increasingly rampant poison flame and boiling resentment from the people. It was proposed at the 33rd regular meeting of the council for detailed discussion, and a unanimous resolution was immediately made: (1) Report to the provincial government and forward it to the central government, ordering Liu Xiang, the commander of the 21st Army in Chongqing, and Wang Lingji, the commander of the 3rd Division of the 21st Army in Wanxian, to prohibit the opening of morphine manufacturing plants. (2) Send letters to Commander Liu and Commander Wang to strictly prohibit manufacturing. (3) Notify all agencies in the city to strictly prohibit sales. (4) Confiscate morphine and punish it at one-half of the original price to be used as a bonus. In addition to separate letters, this case is recorded and submitted to your government for review and approval to strictly prohibit and forward it to the central government to order Liu Xiang, the commander of the 21st Army in Chongqing, and Wang Lingji, the commander of the 3rd Division of the 21st Army in Wanxian, to strictly prohibit it as a public convenience. Based on this, in addition to instructing that the report is known, it is found that morphine and opium are banned together, and the smoking ban law stipulates it clearly. How can they be allowed to set up factories for manufacturing? According to the previous report, in addition to reporting to the central government to instruct the cessation of the establishment of factories for manufacturing and ordering the Ministry of Civil Affairs to inform all counties and cities to strictly prohibit sales, you should know and obey this order. Print and distribute and order the Ministry of Civil Affairs to comply with it. It is reasonable to submit a document to your government for review and approval, ordering the military and political leaders of Sichuan to quickly order their subordinates to stop the opening of morphine manufacturing plants in order to save the people's lives. It is a public convenience, etc. Based on this, it seems that it should be approved as requested. In addition to instructions, a document is prepared and submitted to your government for review and approval, ordering Liu, the commander of the Chongqing Army in Sichuan, to order his subordinates to strictly prohibit it in accordance with the provisions of the smoking ban law and punish them, and forward it to his subordinates to strictly prohibit any further harm."

The Ministry of Finance Requests Regulations on the Scope of Prohibited Exports of Ancient Books

Ancient books have complex editions and are difficult to identify.

Customs officials may find it difficult to implement.

Finance Minister Song Ziwen yesterday presented a special report to the Executive Yuan on the issue of prohibiting the export of ancient books, requesting approval of the prohibited scope. The original text is as follows: "I respectfully received your Yuan's Order No. 2267, stating that the five major cases decided by the Executive Committee of the Chinese Library Association have been examined by the Ministry of Education and their opinions have been added, and the report has been submitted by the Yuan to the National Government for instructions. After checking the attached documents, the Ministry found that the third item, preventing the outflow of ancient books from the country, has been examined by the Ministry of Education to require strict inspections at all ports and transportation agencies to prohibit transportation and export, originally to preserve ancient books. However, our country is the oldest country in terms of culture, and there are many types of circulated printed books. Not only are the books printed in the Song, Yuan, and Ming dynasties the most valuable, but also the various palace editions and rare books printed in the former Qing dynasty are also rarely seen in recent times. Now that we want to prohibit the outflow of nationality from the country, what standard should be used to determine which era's books are prohibited from export? Moreover, the types of editions of books are extremely complex. To distinguish when a book was published and in what era it was printed, only scholars with archaeological expertise can do it. Customs officials may not have this knowledge and will find it difficult to implement. The Ministry believes that it seems that the scope should be clearly defined by your Yuan and it should be stated that in the future, in addition to lithographic, photolithographic, and letterpress printed books being allowed for transportation, all Chinese woodblock printed thread-bound books within the defined scope should be prohibited from being transported out of the country. This is the fundamental way to preserve the national essence, and it will be easier for customs to implement. All reasons for requesting approval of the scope of prohibited export books are reported to your Yuan for review and implementation, and a directive is requested for compliance."

The Situation on the Jiaoji Railway is Tense Again

Qingdao Communication: The Jiaoji Railway war has been in a state of confrontation between the two armies on both sides of the Huai River, west of Zuoshan Station, since the 28th of last month. Neither side has attacked, and it seems to have entered a truce. At present, the Jin army has received a large number of reinforcements, and the Han army is also eager to try because the central reinforcements have arrived. Therefore, the situation has become tense again in the past two days. The two armies are still confronting each other across the Huai River on the front line. The Han army is guarding Zuoshan Station, and the Jin army is between Nanliu and Huangsuobao. After the central reinforcements arrived at the front line, the Han army took over the right wing and handed over the left wing to Li Yunheng's army. At dawn on the 4th, the Jin army came into contact with the Han army again, but the Jin army retreated shortly after the fierce battle. It is expected that there will be a major battle within the next few days. (August 5th)

The Aviation Team Stationed in Hankou Assists in Suppressing Communist Bandits in Hunan and Jiangxi

Hankou Communication: The Aviation Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs has more than ten aircrafts, including fighter planes, reconnaissance planes, and training planes, stationed in Hankou. Recently, several new aircrafts have been added, and the total number of aircrafts is twenty. In addition to most of them being sent to Luohe and Guide to work on the front line, there are still eight fighter planes and reconnaissance planes stationed in Hankou as a reserve team, serving as reconnaissance for the bandit situation in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces, and assisting the army in bombing the communist bandits. Since Changsha was occupied by the communist bandit Peng Dehuai, although the beginning of this month has been cloudy and overcast, making it difficult to fly, the team's planes still bravely advanced and worked hard, reporting the situation obtained from reconnaissance near Changsha and in Pingjiang, Liuyang, Xiaogan, and Huayuan to the Xingying to facilitate military operations. Therefore, Changsha was recaptured within a few days. Today (August 7th) at 6:00 AM, Zhang Yougu, the captain of the 1st Aviation Team, along with pilot Zhong Liren, and pilot Lv Zhenxian, along with Yuan Keming, and Qin Shifan, a pilot of the 5th Aviation Team, along with Dong Shixian, six people drove three new Terkroce aircraft and a Junkers seaplane each, carrying several bombs, and flew separately to Changsha and Pingjiang, Liuyang, Tongcheng, Chongyang, etc. to conduct reconnaissance and bombing. At 12:00 noon, after completing their work in the sweltering heat, they returned to Hankou one after another. According to them, there are no traces of bandits near Changsha at present. The bandits fled in two routes, one towards Pingjiang and Liuyang, and the other towards Liling and Hengshan. Their clothes were disheveled, with gray, blue, black, and white colors. Their appearance was unbearable to look at. The vanguard of our pursuing troops, about a battalion, has tracked them to Ma'anshan. Another regiment of our army crossed the river from Nanjiang Bridge to the west, seemingly pursuing them to Miluo. About four or five hundred fleeing bandits were advancing in a chaotic manner more than ten miles southwest of Yijiawan. When a 60-pound bomb was dropped, the bandits fled in all directions. There were also bandit traces in various villages along the way from Pingjiang to Liuyang, with varying numbers of people. Several villages were burned by the bandits. There were also many bandits in Liuyang City. A bomb was dropped in a temple in the city, which immediately exploded, killing more than a dozen bandits. As for Tongcheng and Chongyang counties, they were all peaceful and there was no bandit situation.

According to Xingying news, because Changsha has been recaptured, the Xiangjiang seaplane of the 5th Aviation Team needs to be stationed in Changsha to conduct reconnaissance of the bandit situation and bombing the communist bandits at any time. Therefore, the team was ordered to send personnel to fly the aircraft there as soon as possible, and instructed them to transport a part of the personnel and oil and ammunition materials to Hunan for replenishment. In addition, in order to prevent unforeseen circumstances and assist the army in severely suppressing them, due to the news that the Zhu-Mao communist bandits were constantly causing disturbances in De'an and Tianjiazhen near Nanchang, it was specially ordered that the 1st and 5th Aviation Teams dispatch three new fighter planes tomorrow morning, carrying bombs, to conduct reconnaissance and bombing in the area near De'an, Qishui, and Chuntianjiazhen. (August 7th)

Rescuing the Declining Value of Jiangxi Circulating Currency

The Department of Finance Convenes Financial Circles and Resolves Seven Measures

Nanchang Dispatch: Due to rampant bandits and poor harvests in Jiangxi, the Department of Finance's income was less than one-tenth or one-twelfth of the budget (monthly budgeted income was about 1.1 million yuan, but actual income was less than 100,000 yuan). Government expenses were heavily in arrears, so the Department issued 1.2 million yuan of circulating currency, using salt surtax as the redemption fund, redeeming about 100,000 yuan each month. Since its issuance in March, it has been redeemed three times, so its use in the market was quite convenient. However, in recent months, the Department of Finance's income has not improved, remaining at around 100,000 yuan per month. In June, the circulating currency fund was diverted to military expenses due to military emergencies, and the currency due could not be redeemed, causing the price to fall daily to 60-70% of its face value. Subsequently, the Department of Finance convened a meeting with business circles and decided that, in addition to the long-term circulating currency (redeemable next year) being sealed up by Yumin Municipal and other banks and various industries, the several hundred thousand yuan circulating in the market would all be treated as cash, and all tax collection agencies must accept it at face value. Therefore, the value of this currency increased daily. However, in the latter half of last month, the communist bandits Zhu De and Mao Zedong captured Zhangshu and Gao'an, and invaded Xishan and Shengmi areas near Nanchang. Public sentiment was unsettled, and the financial sector was the first to be affected. The price of this circulating currency fell daily again. By the 24th and 25th, it could still be used at 60-70% of its face value, but by the end of the month and the beginning of this month, the market completely stopped using it, causing financial chaos. Government employees and ordinary people holding the circulating currency could not buy anything, which was equivalent to waste paper, and everyone was complaining. In recent days, the communist bandits have retreated, and the atmosphere in the provincial capital is better than before. This currency should be used in the market, but various merchants still refuse to use it, using the lack of a redemption fund as an excuse. Some even deliberately close their doors and stop doing business. Although a few stores accept it, prices have skyrocketed several times, and secretly it can only be used at 60-70% of its face value, which has greatly affected the livelihood of the common people. Therefore, the authorities have successively issued announcements by the provincial government and the Martial Law Command, strictly prohibiting discounts and refusals to accept the currency, but to no avail. In order to fundamentally remedy the situation, Director Chen of the Department of Finance will use 200,000 yuan of rice import permits, the share capital of Yumin, Jianshe, and Guohuo Banks, and three months of house and shop rent as the fund for this currency. On the 3rd, he convened a meeting at the General Chamber of Commerce with directors of various industries and the financial sector to discuss maintenance measures. On the 4th, he convened a meeting with leaders of the business and financial sectors to continue the discussion. The following measures were decided: (1) All national and local collection agencies must accept the circulating currency at face value, which will be handled by the Department of Finance. (2) The Department of Finance has stated that in addition to the salt surtax, the share capital of Yumin, Jianshe, and Guohuo Banks, and three months of house and shop rent will be used as the fund. Now, the transfer of ownership of the Zhangguang and Guanghui sections of the city wall foundation is used as collateral to further increase the fund. In addition, each industry will issue notes in accordance with the Beifa loan of 800,000 yuan and deposit them with the Chamber of Commerce for joint responsibility, to be completed within three days. (3) The sealed currency is limited to 400,000 yuan. Half of the previously sealed currency will be returned. The amount that is short will be supplemented by those who have not sealed the full amount, to be completed within three days. If they do not comply, further discussion will be held. (4) The circulating currency is established to rescue finance, and the people have an obligation to assume the circulation of the currency. All transactions must not refuse to accept it. The amount of circulation, excluding the sealed amount, is limited to 400,000 yuan. (5) Change for buying goods is an unavoidable fact. Yumin and Municipal Banks should determine the price and exchange copper coins and banknotes at any time. If copper coins and banknotes are used to exchange, the circulating currency will also be used for payment in and out. (6) The circulating currency for August is allowed to purchase salt from the salt transport bureau and pay the surtax, principal, and interest. (7) The circulating currency should follow the Shanghai banknotes. The exchange settlement office should publicly discuss the exchange rate daily, but it should not be below 95% of its face value. (5th)

The Process of the Guangdong Army Recapturing Guilin

The Majority of the Zhang Guijun Troops Retreat and Gather in Liuzhou and Qingyuan

The Eighth Route Army Dispatches Troops to Assist the Yunnan Army in Attacking Yongzhou

Guangzhou Dispatch: The war in Guangxi Province has been stalled for a long time. Since Chen Jitang went to Wuzhou, he planned to attack Guilin to cut off the enemy's Guiliu transportation, and then attack Liuzhou with all his strength to avoid future troubles. Once the plan was set, he ordered the 59th Division of the front line, Yu Hanmou's troops, the independent brigade of Dong Renhuan's troops, and the 63rd Division of Li Yangjing's troops to each dispatch a part to attack Guilin. On the 25th, they began to move towards their destination. The independent brigade and the Huang Zhiwen brigade of Li's division advanced from Gongcheng and Yangshuo. The Ye Zhao brigade of Yu Hanmou's 59th Division departed from Lipu and met at Gaotian in Liutang. On the 29th, they had opened to Dazhongxu and Liangfengxu areas, only fifty or sixty miles away from Guilin City. At that time, the defending army was the Liang Chaoji Division of the Guilin Army. Three lines of defense were built outside Guilin City. After the Eighth Route Army completed its deployment outside the city, it dispatched five aircraft from Wuzhou to start bombing on the 30th. For two consecutive days, a total of more than 20 heavy 50-pound bombs were dropped. Enemy fortifications near Guilin were all hit and burned. On the 31st, according to aircraft reconnaissance, there were four fires inside and outside the city. The enemy's position was shaken. Therefore, the Yu's and Ye's brigade of the Eighth Route Army, which surrounded the city, ordered an attack at Chenshi on the 1st, and used heavy artillery to cover the infantry's advance. The aircraft circled in the air and dropped bombs to assist in the battle. At this time, the enemy's fortifications had been completely destroyed. After several charges by the Ye's brigade, the enemy was unable to support it and retreated from the north gate in droves. At nine o'clock, the front troops of the Ye's brigade entered the city and searched in different directions. At the same time, they posted notices to reassure the people. In the afternoon, the rear troops, the Huang Zhiwen brigade of Li's division, and the Zeng Youren and Zhang Zhiying regiments of the independent brigade successively entered the city. When attacking Guilin, the Zhang Guijun had once dispatched troops from Baolixu on the evening of the 31st to attack the rear of Yu's division in Xiuren and Lipu. Fortunately, Yu's division had made preparations early and deployed the Li Zhenqiu brigade and the Chen Hanguang regiment to defend. They fought fiercely with the attacking Guijun for two hours. The Guijun was unable to succeed and retreated to Yongfu. After Guilin was captured, the majority of Yu's and Li's divisions opened to Guilin on the 3rd. The Fan Dexing regiment also advanced to Yangshuo. They are now planning to pursue the enemy along the way and attack Liuzhou's military affairs. What the enemy's recent situation is, I think those who are concerned about the current situation also want to know. According to front-line news, Li Zongren of the Guijun is still deploying troops in Liuzhou. The Guijun troops retreating to Liuzhou and the Zhang Fakui troops total about 8,000 to 9,000. However, they are short of funds and equipment. The majority of their troops are deployed in Yongfu, Rongxian, Liuzhou, and Laibin areas. Huang Shaoxiong recently led his troops to Nanning to resist the Yunnan army attacking Yongzhou. Bai Chongxi's troops are in Rongxian. It is said that Liang Chaoji's troops retreated into Lingchuan and Quanzhou after withdrawing from Guilin, and they look like they are fleeing to the Xiang border. In addition to stationing a part of its troops in Guilin to block the enemy's retreat to Xiang, the Eighth Route Army is also rapidly advancing towards Liuzhou with the majority of its troops. At the same time, fearing that they would wipe out one and flee elsewhere, they ordered the Wu Jianhong regiment and the Zhang Jingcheng regiment in the Dahe area to open to Pingnan and Jiangkou to guard the upper reaches of the Dahe, and the newly編edited 16th Brigade of Li Deying's troops to advance to Hengxian to cut off the enemy's rear supply in Nanning, so that the Yunnan army attacking Yongzhou could enter Nanning as soon as possible. (August 4th)

Tragedy at Bengbu Station

Crowded Passengers on the Roof

Nine People Hit by the Overpass and Fall

One Dead and Eight Injured, Very Tragic

Bengbu Dispatch: The Jinpu Railway has recently been insufficient in military vehicles. Ordinary express trains and ordinary additional trains travel back and forth. Soldiers and poor people who do not buy tickets often sit and climb on the roof and bottom of the train, causing frequent dangers. Although the railway bureau has tried its best to prohibit it, in fact there are various difficulties, and the prohibition is ineffective, resulting in traffic delays. Yesterday (4th) at 8 pm, an ordinary express train No. 2 from Pukou had more open-air passengers without tickets on the roof than usual. Therefore, the train arrived at Bengbu Station with a delay of more than three hours. The railway staff saw that there were hundreds of soldiers and civilians sitting indiscriminately on the roof, fearing that danger would occur when the train started. They ordered the railway protection team and police officers to climb up and drive them away. The soldiers still sat firmly, and the old people who had not bought tickets also relied on the soldiers' hometown relationship as a talisman. This drove away that up, and that drove away this up, and it became more and more numerous after a long time of disturbance, even to the point where there was no room for the knee on the roof, or squatting or standing or sitting or lying, and the shapes were not the same. The railway staff saw that there was no way to drive them away, so they had to order the driver to start the train. The train started and approached the overpass after a few steps. Usually, people sitting on the roof of the car under the bridge would lie down on the top of the roof to prevent the bridge railings from colliding. This time there were too many people on the roof and there was no way to bend down. Therefore, when the car passed under the bridge, nine people on the roof were immediately hit by the iron base of the bridge and fell on both sides of the railway tracks. The station was shocked at the time, and the road police rushed forward to rescue. The bloodstains on both sides of the railway were already lying horizontally and vertically. The wife of a poor man, Wang Youde, was hit and injured, and died immediately. Wang Youde and other eight injured people were sent to the Jinpu Railway Hospital at the station by Stationmaster Wu. Today's investigation shows that Wang Youde's wife has been buried by the Public Security Bureau. Four of the injured, Wang Youde's right ear was cut off by the iron base of the overpass, and his eldest son Sanya (four years old) had his scalp cracked and sewn by a doctor. Ren Yongming's right femur was broken and his right shoulder was dislocated. Chen Yuanyi's left clavicle was broken. Wang Youde's second son Yaya and Wang Yongzhong, Zhao Daming, and Cao Shulin were slightly injured. It is heard that two soldiers have been discharged from the hospital, and the death of Wang Youde's wife and the injury of his son and the whole family are the most tragic. (August 5th)

Communist Party Discovered Along the Jidun Line

The Provincial Capital Implements Martial Law

Also, Alarm in Yanji

On the 2nd, Jilin Dispatch: In various parts of northeastern China bordering Russia, Russians are secretly hiding and propagating communism, causing great harm. However, thanks to the close precautions taken by our authorities, no incidents have occurred. Recently, the Chinese and Korean communists in various parts of the Northeast received secret orders from the Third International to hold an uprising on August 1st. Therefore, the communist disturbances this time were a planned action. Now, Shenyang has already issued a strict prohibition.

Report of the Ethnological Group on the Investigation of the Hezhen People

The Hezhen people in Northeast China are scattered in the Jiangyan counties under the jurisdiction of the old Yilan Road in Jilin Province, commonly known as the Hezhen people or the Heijin people, also known as the Fish Skin Tartars. Now they are commonly called the Laodazi, and the Western name is Goryte. This ethnic group is divided into the Songhua River and the Ussuri River factions. The Songhua River faction was编organized into four banners in the eighth year of Guangxu in the former Qing Dynasty. A commander was set up in Gadangtun, four miles away from Fujin County, to rule it. The Ussuri River faction was not 编organized into a banner, so it is also called the Waishan people. The scope of this investigation by the Northeast Tungus ethnic group investigation team of the Institute of Ethnology of the Academia Sinica is limited to the Songhua River faction, from Menggolili in Huachuan County to Qindereli in Fuyuan County (that is, renamed Suiyuan). Within this faction, it can be divided into two parts due to different languages: the He tribe from Menggolili to Futing, and the Qiling tribe from Gadangtun to Qindereli. The former mainly lives by hunting, and the latter mainly lives by fishing. As for the research methods, the team members Ling et al. gathered eight people from the ethnic group who had received primary school education and those who had not received education but were more intelligent after arriving in the lower reaches of the Songhua River, and trained them to assist in the work. The research work is divided into five parts: culture, language, anthropometry, photography, and collection of specimens. In terms of material culture, the methods of fishing and hunting and various machines and tools, as well as various methods of leather making, birch bark utensils, housing equipment, clothing decoration, food and drink, and smoking and drinking hobbies are studied in detail. In terms of spiritual culture, the marriage and funeral rituals, justice, politics and education, songs, dances, myths, stories, and art of the Hezhen are studied, and the shaman religion, which is characteristic of the ethnic group, is especially fully studied. The languages of the Hezhen and Qiling tribes are compared, and the outline of their grammar is obtained. Measurements of men and women are carried out to obtain the results. The Hezhen are of mixed blood of many people, and the Qiling tribe can be compared to the pure race of the Tungus. More than 300 photos were taken, and more than 600 specimens were collected. The local names were recorded in detail, and their uses were carefully studied. The daily necessities, religious gods, art works, and other items of the ethnic group were roughly collected, and they were packed into ten large boxes and transported back to the institute together with the four boxes of stone tools specimens of the ethnic group of the Stone Age discovered in Yilan for research.

At the beginning of the Qing Dynasty, the Hezhen people had more than 400 households, estimating their population at about 3,000. Over the past 300 years, the population has not only not increased, but has gradually decreased. Now there are only more than 500 people left. The reasons are: (1) The ethnic group lives by fishing and hunting and does not know how to farm. Recently, Han Chinese have moved to this land to reclaim wasteland and cut down forests. Their enclosure is shrinking day by day, and the antlers and animal skins obtained from each hunting are almost not enough to supply their lives. (2) Men and women, young and old, aged 17 and above, all like to drink burning wine and smoke opium, which harms their bodies. Therefore, all income and expenditure are mostly wasted on tobacco and alcohol, and life is even more difficult. (3) When there are diseases, they only know how to dance the gods and do not believe in medicine. When plagues are prevalent, entire families die. (4) Women with a little beauty are willing to marry Han Chinese. Statistics show that there are more men than women. (5) Women often suffer from malnutrition and tuberculosis, and it is not easy to give birth. (6) The infant mortality rate accounts for 80% to 90% or more. The above are just a few of the major reasons, and opium smoking is the most important reason. Opium can destroy the country and exterminate the race. The Hezhen people can be a lesson for the Chinese people. The Hezhen, who were once called the Tungus heroic tribe, may disappear from the banks of the Songhua River in a few decades.

In addition to investigating the ethnic group, Ling is also concerned about the issue of transplantation. He carefully studied the soil, rainfall, and climate along the Songhua River in the lower reaches of the Songhua River, and found that it is suitable for planting rice and transplanting Southerners. Now, the rice business is monopolized by Koreans, but the planting methods are improper and rely solely on the thickness of the land without turning the soil. There will be no great hope in the future. If you want rice to develop in the future, you must vigorously encourage Southerners to transplant, but Southerners' transplant to the Northeast has repeatedly failed, such as Hunan people in Yilan and Hubei people in Dalai. Recently, Zhejiang people in Taonan, Southerners' transplant cannot be as easy as Zhili, Henan, and Lu people. People from these three provinces have a history of transplanting outside the customs for three or four hundred years. There are many relatives, friends, and fellow villagers who know each other, so it is easy to settle here. Southerners do not have this advantage, and those who handle the transplant are rashly engaged in it on a whim. There is no full preparation before the event, the immigrants are not adequately trained, and the transplant organization lacks a close organization, and those who are in charge of it do not have the professional knowledge of transplantation, so the result is a waste of money and manpower, and little success is achieved.

Ling et al. left Harbin on the 22nd of last month to contact Heilongjiang for the next survey of the Solun and Oroqen people.

Luo Buzhou's Suspicion of Collusion with the Enemy Case is Sent Back for Retrial

Luo Buzhou, a compradore of the Nanjing Heping Foreign Firm, was reported to the Commander-in-Chief's Political Training Department in November of the 16th year of the Republic of China by more than 380 employees of the firm's foreign branch, stating that Luo had provided the warlord Sun Chuanfang with 200,000 yuan in military pay and Zhang Zongchang with 120,000 yuan in foreign currency, which was suspected of colluding with the enemy. The case was transferred to the Special Court for trial, and then transferred to the Jiangsu High Court for handling in accordance with the law. The original plaintiff's witness was interrogated by the former Judge Ye, and the trial was concluded in September of last year, sentencing Luo Buzhou to five years of imprisonment for the crime of suspicion of collusion with the enemy. Luo stated that he was not satisfied and extended lawyers Li Shirui and Wu Chengyu to appeal to the Supreme Court. Luo Buzhou also provided 10,000 yuan in cash and found Sun Hengji and Yan Xinmao, two porcelain shops in Suzhou, to post bail and await the verdict. The Supreme Court has now ruled that the case be sent back to the High Court for retrial. The High Court is scheduled to hear the case on the morning of yesterday (8th). Zheng Chi, the presiding judge of the Second Criminal Court, summoned Luo Buzhou and the plaintiff representatives Tan Huansheng, Han Delu, Liu Xiaoting, Sun Luyi, Zhang Zhiping, and the witnesses Huang Ziying, Zhou Ziyou, Ye Guihua, Mei Yishao, Zhan Guanghua, and other ten people to the court at 11 am. Judge Zheng, accompanied by prosecutor Sun Xiheng, came to the court to hear the case. The plaintiffs Tan Huansheng and others did not arrive. Then Luo Buzhou and the witnesses Huang Ziying, Zhou Ziyou, etc. were interrogated one by one. The main point was whether Luo Buzhou had invited a wine on the 15th day of the first month of the 16th year of the Republic of China. The witnesses all testified that they only had dinner that day and there were two tables of mahjong, but they did not know anything else. Then lawyers Li Shirui and Wu Chengyu defended him. Judge Zheng ordered that the hearing be adjourned to another date because the plaintiffs did not arrive.

The lake bandits from Haizhou and Henan gangs, notorious for robbing ships and kidnapping for ransom in the Su-area Hengjing Wangye area, are now facing internal strife. Communist Fugitive Zhu Xianglin Arrested

Zhu Xianglin, a Communist leader in his twenties, a native of Nanshiyuan near Anzhen, was a contemporary of the executed Zhu Dingbao and Zhu Genchun. He was wanted by the provincial government, with a reward of 300 yuan offered for his capture. The other day, police detectives Liao Dajin and Hua Yaoxian received a confidential tip that Zhu Xianglin had returned home and was hiding in Meicun, north of the town. Liao and his team immediately went to the village, disguised as locals, and captured him in a small teahouse. He was escorted to the county government for interrogation yesterday.

Request to Retain Overdue Fine in the County

The Wuxi County Government had allocated 20,000 yuan of overdue Caocao (Grain Transport) fines to the county's 1930 budget for civil administration, education, construction, agriculture, and commerce. However, a recent order from the provincial government required the funds to be remitted to the province. County Magistrate Sun, citing the county's dire financial situation, with an outstanding deficit of over 70,000 yuan from 1929 that remained unaddressed, and the already heavily reduced 1930 budget, argued that further reductions were impossible. Remitting the overdue fines would lead to a local financial collapse. The matter was brought before the county administration conference, and it was resolved to present the difficulties to the province for review. The petition was submitted to the provincial government yesterday.

County Magistrate Sun's Resignation Approved

Sun Zuji, the county magistrate of Xiyi, who was transferred from the second section chief of the Department of Civil Affairs last year, has been officially appointed by the National Government for over a year and a half. He has submitted four written requests to the province for resignation but has not been approved. Recently, Sun submitted another resignation. Provincial Chairman Ye, considering Sun's firm intention to resign, presented the resignation to the provincial administrative conference yesterday, which approved the resignation. It is heard that the vacancy will be filled by Pan Zhongjia, the former county magistrate of Hangxian, Zhejiang.

Changzhou

Public Security Bureau Organizes Detective Team

尹鵬, Director of the Wu County Public Security Bureau, concerned about rampant banditry in the four villages, has requested the county government to establish a detective team. He also submitted a budget for start-up and recurring expenses. Magistrate Wu presented the proposal to the county administrative conference on the 7th. The result was a start-up budget of 500 yuan and a recurring monthly budget of 190 yuan. Wang Zemin was appointed team leader, Tang Hongming as deputy team leader, and Zhao Shunbao and ten others as detectives. The team headquarters will be located at the Land God Temple in Yulongguan Lane, and the team was established immediately.

Troops Dispatched to Suppress Bandits

Recent robberies at the border of Wujin and Danyang counties have caused Magistrate Wu to dispatch a police squad to join forces with the Wu-Dan Joint Defense Association to suppress the bandits. A stipend was also allocated for practical use. As robberies have also been frequently reported at the border of Wujin and Jiangyin, Magistrate Wu has also dispatched a team to work with the Wu-Cheng Joint Defense Association to eliminate the bandits within a set timeframe. All police teams have been dispatched.

Nantong

All Circles Comfort Wounded and Sick Soldiers

Nantong City established the 31st Rear Hospital, transporting over 1,600 wounded and sick soldiers. Local representatives, including Zong Weichuan, were selected to visit the hospital to comfort each wounded officer with six silver dollars and each wounded soldier with four silver dollars.

Countywide Anti-Bandit Security

Due to the unsettled atmosphere caused by bandits in Tongyi, the county government has ordered all districts to establish security committees and organize security groups. Pillboxes have been built at all key points, and police squads have been dispatched to guard coastal and river ports. The city and suburbs are maintained by the security forces, and provincial and county police squads are responsible for patrol duties in various districts.

What Was Heard in the Great Thunderstorm in Tongcheng

A severe thunderstorm struck Tongcheng at 6 pm on the 6th, unprecedented in the last twenty years. The thatched house of a Mr. Wang in Gaojiaqiao was struck by lightning, and his wife was electrocuted and died. The Wenfeng Pagoda in the south of the city was partially destroyed by lightning. A corner of the Liminfang in the city center was also collapsed.

Reduction of County Education Funds

Due to banditry, the local tax revenue in Nantong has decreased. The Bureau of Education has submitted a proposal to the Education Administration Committee to reduce the county's education funds for the 15th year by 36,000 yuan from last year's budget. The new budget is listed as 278,421 yuan.

Jiangyin

[P Continuing Dispatch of Wounded Soldiers Temporarily Suspended

Commander Yang and Magistrate Li of the Fortress, along with various agencies of the county party headquarters, wired the authorities for instructions and reported everything on the 4th due to the importance of local security, and ruffians looted the guns of military police in the downtown area, fired guns and disrupted the social order. Following receipt of the telegram yesterday (7th), Commander Yang is responsible for local security and will punish those who disrupt the order according to law. In addition, the agencies of the county party headquarters, as Jiangyin is a small and remote place, the 25th Rear Hospital has accommodated more than 500 wounded soldiers, and a telegram was sent to the Military Medical Department of the Headquarters to waive the continued dispatch to Cheng. Yesterday, a reply telegram was received that the continued dispatch has been temporarily suspended. The wounded soldiers who have recovered will also telegraph the director Wu Yun'an to find out and transport them to the front.

Three Bandits Captured in Western Townships

Magistrate Li, in view of the severity of banditry in the western townships, convened a meeting of the security corps of the eastern and southern townships the night before last and led a team to the townships to search through Licheng, Huangshan, Huangcun and other places. Three bandits, Liu Hongxi, Sun Dexiang and Wang Tianxi, were captured in Xiguanzhuang Village and returned to the city in the rain on the evening of the 6th.

The Construction Department of Jiangsu Province built a wall that encroached on civilian land. Various groups petitioned for its demolition, and the County Party Committee also sent a letter to the Construction Department asking for its early removal to appease public opinion. The Construction Department made no response, causing public uproar. The County Executive Committee issued an official letter yesterday convening various agencies and groups to hold a meeting at the Assembly Hall of the Committee at 2 pm today (8th) to publicly discuss solutions as a final resolution.

Undercurrents Regarding the Selection of the Director of the Education Bureau

Since the resignation of Han Wenqing, the Director of the Zhenjiang Education Bureau, there have been many local figures vying for the position, with a certain Mr. Liu being the most vocal. People in the education sector are quite dissatisfied with this news and are collectively opposing it. They plan to petition the authorities to dismiss the idea of Mr. Liu taking over the Education Bureau to avoid unexpected turmoil.

Yangzhou

Urging the Reorganization of the Chamber of Commerce

The county government, citing the Chamber of Commerce Law promulgated by the National Government on August 15, 1929, which required Chambers of Commerce established before the promulgation of the law to reorganize within one year, and repeated urging from the provincial government, has ordered the County Chamber of Commerce and the Xianshaoguayi, Daqiao Chambers of Commerce to reorganize on schedule to comply with the law.

Unfilial Son Injures His Biological Father

Bu Zheng'an, a resident of Xiajiazhuang, north of Xinjiaqiao in Shangshuishi, county, was beaten to death by his son, Bu Xiaoshi. Long Xiang, a nephew of the deceased, and Xu Xialin, who guaranteed him, locked Xiaoshi next to the body. Later, the town head, Xu Hongxun, released Xiaoshi secretly in the middle of the night. The county, based on reports from Wang Zhiguo, the deputy town head, and others from the 10th Autonomous District, that the unfilial son had harmed his parent and violated moral principles, requested an investigation. Yesterday (6th), the district head was instructed to inform the relatives of the deceased that the case involved human life and should be directly filed with the court for investigation, as it was not within the scope of administrative matters.

Prohibition of Collecting Tolls at the Wuyu Wharf

The Wuyu Wharf toll in Sima Town, a township in the county, was created by the late village elder Wang Shaonan. The county, based on a petition from the Sima Branch of the Commercial and Administrative Association requesting a prohibition, ordered the relevant 5th District Office to investigate and respond. Yesterday (5th), the district office replied to the county that Wang had passed away many years ago, and no one was responsible for the accounts, making it impossible to investigate. The county government immediately issued a prohibition based on the report.

Twists and Turns in the Trafficking Case

The Public Security Bureau of the county previously investigated and found Wang Buhai, a trafficker, and the girl abducted from Fanchuan at the Bo'ai Hospital on Zuowei Street in the city. After the suspect was proven and bailed out, a Mr. Wang discovered that the girl had other relationships with the Bo'ai Hospital. Yesterday evening (6th), he went to the hospital to make a big noise, causing a conflict with Zhang Liran's younger brother, Zu, the director of the hospital. Both sides were taken to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau. After a lawyer intervened, they were temporarily released on bail. When this was known to Tang, the section chief of the Judicial Section of the General Bureau, he immediately telegraphed the First Branch of the Bureau to quickly arrest the two suspects and send them to the Bureau for transfer to the judicial authorities for handling.

Increasingly Bizarre Extortion

A resident of Tangzi Lane in the city, Yao Zhizhi, received a threatening letter a few days ago, demanding twenty yuan and specifying that the money should be placed in the middle of a large plaster, which should then be affixed to the right side of his family's front door. Yao himself works in Shanghai. His wife, being timid, dared not speak out and followed the instructions. The next morning, the plaster on the wall had disappeared. A few days later, another letter arrived, lowering the price by five yuan and instructing him to do the same. The matter was known to Yao Zhibi's elder brother, Zhixi, who strongly dissuaded his sister-in-law from complying and planned to report it to the police district. His sister-in-law, fearing resentment, secretly prepared five yuan and did as instructed. This is truly a strange phenomenon of increasingly bizarre extortion.

The rice prices in Hangzhou have not decreased, but been manipulated by rice merchants, despite the new rice entering the market from all directions. Huzhou

Wu Arong's Home Robbed by Bandits

Wu Arong, a resident of Changxing, about three miles outside the East Gate of Huzhou, is a wealthy man whose home has long been coveted by bandits. In the winter of the year before last, Arong's son was kidnapped by bandits and redeemed for a thousand yuan. Unexpectedly, at about 9 pm on the 4th of this month, more than ten bandits, speaking with a Henan accent and carrying firearms, broke down the door. The family members fled through the back door upon hearing the news. The bandits entered and searched everywhere but found no one. They robbed Wu's family of all clothing, foreign goods, and ornaments, firing several shots into the air as they left.

Zhu Luo Amei, a notorious bandit (a company commander under Taibao Ashu), haunts places such as Luwan Temple, Qijiantou, and Xinmiao Town in the eastern townships, acting without restraint in broad daylight. Shangyu

Disaster Caused by Fengshui at Caojiang and Houhai

The coastal villages in this county, located along the former river and sea, are situated in low-lying areas that are prone to flooding during continuous rains. The villages along the Cao'e River, including Sanjie, Zhangzhen, Xiaojiang, Zhangcun, Pukou, Fengjiapu, Xiajiabu, Shangpu, Hengting, Jiazhai, Kunlun, Huapu, Haoba, and Nanxue, have been suffering from continuous heavy rain since the 20th of last month, followed by a hurricane. The river tide rose, and the waters of Xinshan and the streams in the county converged and rushed down, inundating all the crops planted on the riverfront sand. All harvested rice straw, livestock, chickens, geese, etc., were swept away by the rushing waves, especially in the villages of Fengjiapu and Xiajiabu, where boats could navigate between the fields without hindrance. It is said that the tide suddenly rose on the 31st of the morning, causing the ferry to stop for five or six hours. In addition, most of the residents in Songxia Houhai make a living by fishing and planting cotton, corn, and mildew beans. This time, they suffered damage from floods and hurricanes, totaling three to four thousand acres, worth more than ten thousand yuan.

Ningbo

Three Robberies

(1) Yesterday afternoon at 7 pm, six bandits, armed with wooden cases, suddenly entered the Huisui Rice Store in Wanjia Bridge, Dongguan District, Zhenhai, and robbed the store's cash register of 123 silver dollars. Three members of the local defense corps were stationed there, but they were outnumbered and dared not resist, only firing a few shots into the air, allowing the bandits to escape. Neighboring shops were spared from the robbery. (2) The family members of Lu Shengqing, the director of the Yaojiang Hospital in the northern township of Yuyao, also lived in the hospital. The night before last at 8 pm, seven robbers suddenly came. Two bandits guarded the door, while the others entered the room and ransacked the trunks and cabinets, robbing them of more than 200 yuan in silver, thirteen gold rings, and dozens of pieces of clothing. After the robbery, they fired shots in the air to intimidate. (3) Shaobai Ridge in Yindong is the thoroughfare from Ningbo to Tiantong Temple. At about 1 pm on the 5th of this month, a young woman, about twenty years old, was on her way from Ningbo to Tiantong Street to visit a friend. When she passed Shaobai Ridge, she suddenly encountered a bandit who grabbed her. Knowing the danger, the woman immediately took out five yuan from her pocket and gave it to the bandit. The bandit took the money with one hand and pushed the woman to the ground, robbing her of a gold bracelet and an umbrella.

Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education Revises Service Regulations for Principals of Experimental Elementary Schools in Jiangsu Province

The Ministry of Education instructed the Jiangsu Education Department to revise the service regulations for principals of experimental elementary schools in Jiangsu Province. The order stated that the submitted documents have been reviewed (the service regulations for principals of provincial secondary schools are satisfactory). The general direction is approved and recorded. However, certain provisions in the service regulations for principals of provincial experimental elementary schools and secondary schools are cumbersome. Provisions 1, 2, and 3 are particularly difficult to implement in practice. Since principals are responsible for all duties in their schools and also hold positions in the secondary school normal course, how can they find time to travel to each county for an inspection every year? Therefore, the following revisions should be made: (1) Each year, use holidays or other times to convene a local education bureau chief or inspector, and elementary school representatives from each county to conduct an education research meeting. Discuss the actual problems of elementary schools, report on the experimental results of the school, and guide elementary schools in each county to improve and progress. Submit the minutes and resolutions of the meeting to the Education Department for verification. (2) When necessary, visit each region and county to inspect local education, report experimental results, and give educational speeches to guide elementary schools in each county to improve and progress. Submit the inspection results to the Education Department for verification. Provisions 4 and 5 are changed to Provisions 3 and 4. Provision 6 is deleted. You are required to comply with the revisions and resubmit the revised regulations to the Ministry for verification.

Further News on the Shanghai Private School Screening Examination

The screening examination for graduates and students of unregistered and closed specialist schools and above in Shanghai City, which is being organized by the Ministry of Education to help unemployed youth, has been scheduled to be held on the 17th, 18th, and 19th at Jiaotong University in Xujiahui. Each student must take eight to ten subjects, with each subject lasting two hours. It is scheduled to be completed in three days. The application deadline is set for the 10th, which is only two days away and will not be extended. There are especially many law students who have signed up.

Meeting Proceedings

After a group photo was taken, the attendees filed into the venue. The meeting was presided over by Zhu Shaoping, the Secretary-General of the World Chinese Students' Federation. Chen Dezheng, the Director of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, served as chairman and began with formal salutations. Chairman Chen then delivered a farewell speech, stating that the hope of the seventeen groups in Shanghai for everyone was even stronger than in the past, because the economic burden of going abroad for students was not as heavy as it is today. Since the price of gold has risen, the economic burden on both publicly funded and privately funded students has approximately doubled. Therefore, everyone's responsibilities have increased, and the hopes of the various groups for everyone have also become greater. Our country sends hundreds of students abroad every year, and quite a few return home. But society does not appear to be affected at all. Is the country and society not using talent? Or are the people unwilling or unable to contribute to the country and society? This is the question. In the past, graduates of higher primary schools and secondary school students also went abroad to study, which was too uneconomical. Now that this trend has been reduced, the government should establish large-scale academic research institutions to provide specialized research for those in the country who have received higher education, and it is not necessary to take so much money abroad to study. But the current situation does not allow you to travel far away at this expensive time, and your ambition is commendable. I sincerely hope that this time you go abroad, you can use this perseverance and spirit to extract the essence of that country to build a new China in the future. After that, Mr. Anlide, the Commercial Counselor of the American Embassy, spoke, stating that Mr. Zhu Shaoping of the Global Chinese Students' Federation has given the attention that you need to pay to everything when going to the United States. I do not want to say more. Now I would like to ask you to pay attention to two things: First, after arriving in the United States, you must communicate with Americans from time to time. Do not be lonely and self-reliant. Second, if you are not familiar with the route or have difficulties, you must ask more people to avoid suffering yourself. After Mr. An's speech, Mr. Biren Xijiu gave a speech, stating that Chinese culture occupies an extremely important position in the world. I sincerely hope that after arriving in Europe, you will not only work hard in your studies but also pay attention to the characteristics of Western culture in order to promote China's inherent culture. After the speech, Mr. Tan Boyu, the representative of Tongji University, gave a speech, saying that all the points of hope that we people have for you have been said by Chairman Chen one by one. I do not want to discuss more. I want to contribute to you now, that is, when you go abroad to study, you must be determined to study a certain subject. Those who study engineering must learn the smaller scale industries that are suitable for China's economic environment. Determination has its own experience, and learning small-scale industries is more suitable for the current situation in China. These two points are what I hope you will pay attention to. After Mr. Tan finished speaking,

The Municipal Education Bureau Regularly Inspects Private School Teachers

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Measures for Improving Private Schools

The following five regulations have been established for the inspection of private school teachers. Inspections will be conducted regularly according to the following methods: (1) All private school teachers in this city must register with the bureau. (2) Registration will be open from August 10th to August 25th. (3) When registering, teachers must fill out their name, age, place of origin, resume, and the address of the private school, and submit two recent 2.5-inch portrait photos. (4) The inspection will be held on September 1st and 2nd at the Municipal Wuben Girls' Middle School on Huangjia Road. (5) The inspection will consist of three parts: a physical examination, an oral examination, and a written examination. The written examination will cover: (1) Party Principles, (2) Mandarin, (3) Arithmetic, (4) General Knowledge.

Pre-announcement of the White Goose Painting Society Exhibition

The White Goose Painting Society was founded in the spring of the 17th year of the Republic by famous painters Fang Xuejiu, Pan Sitong, Dou Xueou, and Chen Qiucao. It has been reorganized several times. Although the group has not had significant public exposure, it has been working very hard internally. Because they did not want to indiscriminately gather members and ruin the original spirit, Chen, Fang, Pan, and Dou contributed funds to create the White Goose Painting Research Institute, sacrificing their time and energy to focus on cultivating real talent and promoting the true spirit of art research. After a year, many talents have emerged. In order to complete unification, the society has actively collected and selected members such as Feng Qiuhen and Zhou Xi to prepare for the first painting exhibition in Shanghai. At the same time, they are expressing their initial intention to engage in pure artistic movements. It is said that the exhibition date will be in the cool autumn month of September, and all arrangements will be carefully designed. It is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time.

New Information from the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center

The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center has recently paid special attention to guidance for further education during employment guidance and psychological testing. The publication of special issues is quite relevant to the needs of young people seeking further education in various places. Recently, in response to requests from young people in various places, it is investigating the entrance examination questions of various universities and middle schools and publishing them in the "Further Education Guide" to help young people prepare for the examinations. To serve young people in terms of guidance, service, and self-cultivation, it has published "Vocational Guidance Lectures," priced at 12 cents per booklet, available at the center and the Civilization Bookstore. In order to meet the needs of all sectors of society, it has consulted with the China Vocational Education Society to establish specialized courses in clerical work, phonetic symbols, and worker education teacher training in a trial basis to create specialized talents for social application. Recent statistics show that an average of 40 people come to the center for consultations daily, an average of 20 people register, an average of 10 people seek further education, and about four or five people entrust the center with their cases. However, only about one-tenth of the introductions are successful. Yesterday, Jilin University sent a telegram requesting the introduction of a professor of law and politics. The center immediately introduced Dr. Wei Liangsheng. A middle school in this city entrusted the center to hire a registrar who must be proficient in English and Chinese, diligent, and capable, with a monthly salary of 40 yuan. Those who wish to apply must first send their Chinese and English works and handwriting samples to the center. A girls' middle school in Anhui Province entrusted the center to introduce a female teacher of embroidery and sewing and a female teacher of knitting socks, towels, and undershirts, both with rich experience and over 25 years of age, with a monthly salary of 60 yuan each.

At the end of the game, the audience applauded again, as if celebrating Nanhua's success.
