However, the generally well-meaning people in the neighborhood all said that the parturient woman was frightened and closed her breath, and her heart was still warm and could be cured. Unexpectedly, the neighbors did not wait for the consent of the family and immediately invited Jiangbei female doctors Chen Cai and Zhou Zhang to come. The family members who witnessed the tragic situation were even more悲愤. Detective Wang Disguised as a Representative

A Password Apprehends Three People

Joint Shanghai-Moganshan Transportation Service

Trains, Automobiles, and Mountain Sedan Chairs

Implementation on the 10th of This Month

In the past, tourists traveling between Shanghai and Moganshan purchased joint transportation tickets from the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway for trains, steamboats, and mountain sedan chairs. Since the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau's buses have reached Shou Village, taking a bus from Hangzhou to Shou Village and then switching to a sedan chair to ascend the mountain has become faster than using steamboats. As a result, the steamboat business has implicitly been eliminated. However, there was no joint transportation arrangement between trains and automobiles. It was extremely inconvenient for passengers traveling to and from the mountain from Shanghai to carry luggage and belongings. Recognizing this, the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway negotiated a joint train-automobile-mountain sedan chair transportation contract with the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau in the spring of this year. After repeated consultations, the agreement was finally settled recently and is scheduled to be implemented on August 10th. For those traveling from Shanghai to the mountain, take the second train departing from the North Station at 7:00 AM or the fourth train departing at 9:00 AM on the Shanghai-Hangzhou line to Hangzhou. Then, transfer to a bus to Shou Village, and finally switch to a mountain sedan chair to ascend the mountain. For those traveling from the mountain to Shanghai, take a mountain sedan chair to Shou Village, transfer to a bus to Hangzhou, and then take the third train departing from the City Station at 9:50 AM or the ninth train departing at 6:05 PM on the Shanghai-Hangzhou line to Shanghai. Fixed seats are reserved on the trains to match the number of joint transportation tickets sold, so there will be no temporary seat shortages. All detailed information and procedures for purchasing round-trip joint transportation tickets can be obtained by contacting the information desk at the North Railway Station. From now on, luggage and belongings can be transported directly, which is truly good news for travelers.

British Elderly Woman Celebrates Birthday Today

Mrs. Baldwin, the Oldest Foreign Resident in Shanghai

According to the "Great American Evening Post," Mrs. Baldwin, a British resident of this city, will hold a grand Chinese banquet tomorrow (the 9th) to celebrate her 90th birthday. Mrs. Baldwin was born in 1840. She is not only the oldest among the foreign residents but also the one who has resided in Shanghai for the longest time. She came to Shanghai sixty-seven years ago to marry Mr. Baldwin. After several voyages with her husband, he passed away in South America. Mrs. Baldwin returned to her home country once, but then came back to Shanghai, where she has remained for fifty-eight years without ever traveling elsewhere. She told reporters that she already considers Shanghai her hometown. If she were to return to her home country now, she would not recognize anyone, and it would feel like going to a foreign land. Therefore, she intends to spend her remaining years in Shanghai.

Hu Lianquan, a Native of Chuanshan, Proposes the Construction of the Chuanshan Guildhall

Direct Transportation of Coffins... To Benefit the Poor and Provide Convenience

Letters Sent to Fellow Townsmen in Shanghai... Seeking Sponsorship to Make It Happen

Chuanshan Town, under the jurisdiction of Zhenhai County, serves as the main entrance and exit for the three townships of Yan, Tai, and Hai under Zhenhai County, and the two townships of Xie Nan and Xie Bei under Dinghai County. Tens of thousands of Chuanshan natives reside in Shanghai. In the past, when people from Chuanshan Town returned to their hometown, they had to detour through Ningbo. Even coffins from bereaved families had to pass through the Siming Public Association in Ningbo. The detour had no impact on affluent families in Chuanshan, but it caused great inconvenience and suffering to impoverished bereaved families. Since the establishment of direct shipping between Shanghai and Chuanshan, transportation has become more convenient, and there is no need to detour through Ningbo. However, the transportation of coffins still follows the previous practice without any changes. Recently, Mr. Hu Lianquan, a Chuanshan native who works for the Shanghai Sanbei Steamship Company, often saw fellow townsmen and women crying and supporting coffins at the docks while traveling between Shanghai and Chuanshan for work. This was especially common during the Qingming and Winter Solstice festivals. Moved by what he saw, Mr. Hu asked about the reasons and learned about the inconvenience of detouring coffins and the inability to afford transportation costs. Moved by this information, Mr. Hu proposed to follow the example of Dinghai by purchasing land in Chuanshan and building a Chuanshan Guildhall and subsidiary buildings so that bereaved families of impoverished Chuanshan natives in Shanghai could directly transport coffins back to their hometown. This would provide convenience and save transportation costs. However, Mr. Hu felt that the matter was too significant for him to accomplish alone. He drafted a proposal outlining the current situation and facts regarding the transportation of coffins, as well as the need for and benefits of the construction project. He earnestly requested sponsorship from the prominent businessman Yu Qiaqing to facilitate the early completion of the project. After reading the proposal, Mr. Yu greatly admired it and agreed to provide sponsorship in person. He also instructed Mr. Hu to first seek the support of fellow Chuanshan natives and business leaders in Shanghai to jointly contribute to the charitable cause. Therefore, Mr. Hu has now joined forces with fellow townsman Mr. Hu Zhizhai to begin soliciting support. It is expected that fellow Chuanshan natives, who care about their hometown, will fulfill their duty and jointly work together to achieve the project early and benefit impoverished fellow townsmen.

Continuing Report on the Guo Ju'an Appeal Case

Guo Ju'an and the American Chase Bank are involved in a lawsuit concerning a guarantee dispute. Dissatisfied with the first instance judgment, Guo Ju'an filed an appeal. The details of the trial proceedings have been reported by this newspaper. It has been learned that Chaozhou merchant groups have paid significant attention to this case. It is also understood that, in addition to citing "the lack of standing of foreign legal persons" in the appeal petition, the petition also states that the appeal in the first instance was illegal. Further details are provided as follows: (Defense of Rightful Restraint: In litigation, the defense of rightful restraint refers to a situation where, during the continuation of a lawsuit, another lawsuit is filed with the same parties, the same cause of action, and the same subject matter, seeking the same claim, either through a principal lawsuit or a counterclaim. If the lawsuit has already been restrained, a defense of obstruction can be raised based on rightful restraint. According to Article 294 of the Code of Civil Procedure, the restraint of litigation begins with the filing of the lawsuit. In the first instance of this case, the appellant was the defendant. Before the appellee filed the lawsuit on May 15th, the appellant had already filed a lawsuit against Zhang Songzhou, the compradore of Chase Bank, on May 10th, listed as General No. 5255 of the 18th year. Because the appellant filed the lawsuit before the appellee, rightful restraint naturally arises according to the rules of litigation. The appellee cannot file another lawsuit based on the same cause of action. However, the first instance judge failed to examine the provisions of Article 295 of the Code of Civil Procedure, which state that a party cannot file another lawsuit concerning a matter under litigation restraint. Instead, the judge dismissed the plaintiff's (i.e., the appellee's) claim based on Article 290, Section 6 of the Code of Civil Procedure. The appellant had already clarified this point in the original trial, but the trial judge did not make a ruling. Therefore, the appellee's lawsuit in the first instance was actually illegal and should be resolved first.)

This newspaper reported yesterday that the British-owned Brunner Mond & Co. had specially made a balloon for aerial advertising and attempted to release it from the platform on the third floor of the Yufeng Cigarette Paper Store at No. 393 Avenue Edward VII in the International Settlement. After investigation by the police, no evidence was found, so no charges were filed. Subsequently, the police transferred him to the Second Branch of the Higher Court, which then transferred him to the Shanghai Special District Local Court due to jurisdictional issues. He is currently still in custody. Wu is usually honest and cautious in his service at the newspaper and has no reactionary tendencies. They are requesting the association to appeal on his behalf so that he can be exonerated. Zhang Genlin Illegally Detains Wife

Shackles Her Feet and Locks Her in a Dark Room

The Township Police Detect and Arrest Him for Investigation

Zhang Genlin, a villager from the Shenjiaxiang Huatingtou area of the Yinxiang District in the northeastern part of this county, is known for his violent temper. His wife, Zhang Xu (also known as Xu Xiuling), is often abused by her husband and is even deprived of food all day long. Therefore, she fears her husband like a tiger. Zhang Xu was betrothed to Zhang Genlin by her grandmother when she was seven years old. They were married in the winter of 1928. However, after less than two months, Zhang was unable to support her and sent her back to her mother's home. All of Zhang Xu's dowry was pawned off by Zhang Genlin to support his extravagance. To make a living, Zhang Xu had no choice but to work in a factory to support herself. In July of this year, Zhang Genlin planned to sell Zhang Xu. Zhang Xu refused, so Zhang Genlin hated her intensely. In late June, he shackled Zhang Xu's feet with large shackles and locked her in a dark room, depriving her of food for ten days. The patrol police from the Military Industry Road Police Station of the First Division of the Seventh District learned about this. On the night before last, they went to the address and heard a woman crying inside. They knocked on the door and entered, finding a woman huddled in a corner, weeping, with a gaunt face and emaciated body. They asked her what was wrong and learned that she was Zhang Xu. They checked her feet and found that she was still wearing shackles. The police immediately arrested Zhang Genlin, but he had already fled. They took Zhang's father, Zhang Songbao, and the victim, Zhang Xu, to the police station (without removing the shackles). Zhang Jiguang, the police chief, investigated the case and learned that Zhang Xu had been subjected to repeated abuse. Zhang was furious that Zhang Genlin dared to possess illegal instruments of torture and impose private punishments, disregarding the law. He immediately ordered the police to arrest Zhang Genlin and bring him in for investigation. He also temporarily detained Zhang Songbao and Zhang Xu, pending a formal report to the headquarters and transfer to the court for thorough investigation.

New Couple Argue for Divorce

Lu Fubao and Wu Caizhang

Lu Fubao, a woman from Pudong, and her husband, Wu Caizhang, recently had disagreements. Lu Fubao hired lawyer Chen Jinrong to file a petition with the Local Court requesting a divorce. Her petition stated that the marriage was based on deception with the intention of obtaining property and requested the annulment of the marriage contract to protect her personal rights and recover her losses. The plaintiff, without parents or siblings, had been living comfortably on her late husband's inheritance for several years. However, due to the rising cost of living, it was difficult to sustain her lifestyle. She intended to remarry to provide for her basic needs. Xu Qing's wife seized the opportunity and introduced her to the defendant, Wu Caizhang. Through various sweet-talking methods, they entered into a marriage contract and lived together. Within a month, the plaintiff's clothes and ornaments had been pawned off, and she was subjected to poor treatment. Therefore, she requested the annulment of the fraudulent marriage contract and the recovery of losses amounting to 274 yuan. The defendant, Wu Caizhang, also hired lawyer Huang Yiyan to file a response, stating that, because he was unmarried, he had married the plaintiff on the sixth day of the third lunar month of this year through a matchmaker, Xu Qing's wife, a friend of his brother. The bride price was agreed to be 200 yuan and a silk dress. Initially, they lived in harmony, but after a month, the plaintiff's behavior changed. She often went out, and he repeatedly advised her against it, but she ignored him. On July 5th, she secretly took away her valuables and clothes, indicating her intentions. Now, she has suddenly filed for divorce, clearly because she has found another lover. The defendant has already spent about 400 yuan on marrying the plaintiff, and they have only been married for four months. How can the marriage contract be dissolved? He cannot ignore the sacrifices of others. He requested the court to consider the difficulty of poor people marrying and to order them to live together. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, Judge Tong Shenglv specially opened the Second Courtroom for the trial. The plaintiff, Lu Fubao, testified that she was 28 years old, a local resident of Yipin Lane, Baoshan Road, Zhabei, No. 234, and recounted the previous events, requesting the annulment of the marriage contract. The defendant, Wu Caizhang, testified that he was 32 years old, a Ningbo native living on Baoshan Road, and worked as a headman at a dance hall. He did not want to separate and requested to live together, and also recounted the events. The judge, considering it necessary to call witnesses, ordered both parties to appear in court again at 8:00 AM the next day (i.e., today) for continued trial and instructed the defendant to invite his mother and sister to court for verification.

The Henan Relief Association's Aid to War-Affected Civilians

Mr. Zhou Xiwen, the representative of the Henan Provincial Relief Association stationed in Shanghai, recently received a telegram from the provincial capital, which is recorded as follows: "To all charitable organizations in Shanghai: According to a report from Luo Chuanming, the Magistrate of Qi County, the county has fallen into a war zone, and all grain, fodder, carts, horses, and laborers have been requisitioned by various armies, resulting in extreme hardship. The war has raged within the county for 43 days, destroying countless houses, and people have died in large numbers. As a result, the wheat has not been harvested, and corpses are scattered across the fields, unable to be buried. Those who survived the catastrophe are crying out for food. Qi County is located in a strategic location, and the war has been particularly fierce. The losses suffered by the people are incalculable, and those who have died or been displaced urgently need rescue. We earnestly hope that all philanthropists will show great compassion and provide extensive relief. Respectfully, Li Shican, Chairman of the Henan Provincial Relief Association." After receiving the telegram, Representative Zhou went to various charitable organizations in Shanghai to present the situation of the disaster and plead for immediate relief.

The Jisheng Society Continues to Allocate Loans for the Minsheng Branch Canal

The Minsheng Canal in Qi County, Henan Province, which is funded by the China Jisheng Society, is 40 li long and can irrigate thousands of acres of fertile land, generating significant profits. The canal project has now been completed. The total investment is more than 80,000 yuan. Qi County has raised and the government has allocated a total of about 50,000 yuan. The Society has loaned 30,000 yuan. This huge project is generating substantial profits. According to a legal estimate, even if it cost 200,000 or 300,000 yuan, it would be worth it. Now, it has been completed for only 80,000 yuan. The reason is that using labor for relief is twice as effective, and the workers are mostly experienced and skilled, with some who are willing to sacrifice their families to alleviate the disaster. As a result, good results have been achieved. The work has been inspected and found to be solid and reliable, and the waterway is convenient and beneficial to the fields. However, in many places where branch canals have been opened, there are still outstanding wages for completed work. Because Qi County has accumulated deficits over the years and cannot borrow money, the original handler of the project negotiated a loan contract with the Society. Mr. Dong Junhengqu, the person in charge, wrote to request a loan of 2,000 yuan to pay for the labor of repairing the scattered branch canals, which would further improve them. The Society agreed that the water conservancy project would be beneficial for hundreds of years. Since this small amount of outstanding wages cannot be resolved due to the years of famine, it is sincere and earnest to negotiate with the Society for a loan. They have to work together to help others. It has been agreed to continue to loan 2,000 yuan for labor relief, which will be remitted soon.

The Chinese Buddhist Pilgrimage and Sightseeing Group

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday from Tianjin

Staying at Lingshan Temple

The Chinese Buddhist Pilgrimage and Sightseeing Group arrived in Shanghai yesterday from Tianjin on the Fengtian wheel. The travelers are staying at Lingshan Temple outside the Dananmen Gate in this city. It is said that the purpose of the group is to inspect the current situation of Buddhist education and the thoughts and lives of Buddhists in various Buddhist countries in East Asia. The aim is to connect Buddhist culture at home and abroad and to unite Buddhists around the world. The trip is scheduled to last for three years. They are now in Shanghai to handle travel matters. Once everything is ready, they will start their journey. The group's travel plan is briefly recorded as follows: (1) Japan, (2) Siam, (3) Myanmar, (4) India, etc.

Ning Shao Company Expands Business to Include Water, Fire, and Life Insurance

Petition to the Bureau of Social Affairs

In addition to its shipping business, the Ning Shao Company in this city has had a ship water and fire insurance department for many years, which has been quite successful. Recently, its shareholders decided to establish separate water, fire, and life insurance companies. The general manager of the company, Yuan Lidung, submitted a special petition to the Bureau of Social Affairs yesterday, stating that the company has accumulated 250,000 national currency in ship insurance. After discussion by the shareholders, it was decided to set aside 125,000 yuan to establish a water and fire insurance company and to use the remaining 125,000 yuan to establish a life insurance company, following the example of Sincere Company. This is because it is easier to set up a department under a company, and the shareholders remain the same. The general manager is the company's director and supervisor, like the advanced countries. Also, companies such as Swire, Mitsui Bussan of Japan, and others in this city have established other businesses as subsidiaries. China's industry is still young. In addition to Wing On and Sincere, there are no other successors. Therefore, in addition to operating the shipping business, the company plans to add water, fire, and life insurance companies, still using the name of Ning Shao Merchant Shipping, but with each being an independent entity. However, the company's regulations and the provisional rules of the National Registration Bureau do not have provisions for this type of registration. Therefore, the reasons for the establishment are presented for approval and interpretation so that they can be followed.

Executive Committee Meeting of the Accountants' Association

The Shanghai Accountants' Association held its fifth executive committee meeting yesterday. Commissioner Xi Yushu chaired the meeting as scheduled. Matters discussed: (1) Regarding the members' meeting, it was resolved to seek the opinions of all members in writing on the revision of the association's constitution and hand it over to the executive committee. It was resolved to comply with Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs Order No. 2402 and Ministry of Industry and Commerce Order No. 10438, which require amendments to the following points: (A) Article 11 in its entirety and the phrase "but without voting rights" in Article 38 regarding supporting members should be deleted. It is proposed to comply. (B) Article 42, "The amount of the membership fee should be reduced or remain at 30 yuan as in the old constitution." It is proposed to keep it as it is. (C) In all articles of the original constitution, the word "government," except in Article 5, should be changed to "Ministry of Industry and Commerce" or "Administrative Office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce" in accordance with the Accountants Ordinance to comply with regulations. It is proposed to change the word "government" in Article 10, paragraph 3, and Article 12, paragraph 2, to Administrative Office of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and submit it to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. All other instances should be changed to Ministry of Industry and Commerce. The above items should be recorded and notified to all members for their opinions. Please reply within two weeks, otherwise it will be considered as agreement. (2) A letter was sent to the accounting committee to submit the income and expenditure report for July for review. It was resolved to hand it over to the supervisory committee for review. Art World

Recent Trends in the British Literary Scene

— Ming

There are three major events in the British literary scene this year. First, the sensation caused by war novels across the country; second, the unusually large number of literary figures who have passed away; and third, the good fortune of poets. We will discuss them one by one.

In the spring of this year, several new war novels were published in Britain. The best one is probably "Her Privates We" (the meaning of these three words is only understood by British soldiers, and we respectfully decline to translate them). It is said to be the best war novel in the world, even better than "All Quiet on the Western Front." However, so far only Britain (excluding Ireland) is excited about this book. The author is anonymous and uses the pseudonym "Private I9022."

Later, a capable young writer and publisher came out to oppose him. He published a pamphlet saying that everyone treats the events of the war as a nightmare rather than as a part of history. This is not right. This pamphlet actually caused some influence. Subsequently, in daily newspapers, weekly newspapers, and radio broadcasts, a group of nightmare supporters and history supporters debated with each other and took pride in it. As a result, there was still no conclusion. As for the greatest British war novel, it has not yet been produced, and no one knows whether it will be produced in the future. However, everyone now feels a bit annoyed by this question.

The Death of Lawrence

Was not an unexpected event because he had been seriously ill for a long time. However, British public opinion is very divided on his criticism. Some scold him as a nymphomaniac, while others praise him as unprecedented. Both are biased. In fairness, he was indeed a genius. However, there are many narrow and bitter places in his later works, which inevitably reduce the artistic value of the works themselves. Locke (W.J. (Locke), a romantic novelist who was good at writing about circus characters and French life, is also a newly deceased British literary figure. His works are numerous and very popular. They have some interest but no profound meaning, so he can only be considered a second- or third-rate writer.

Two Female Novelists

Have passed away. One is Romer Wilson, the wife of Edward Obrien, an American short story editor. Her death was not mentioned in newspapers or publications. However, there was a time, a few years ago, when she was very prominent and was considered the most promising young female writer in Britain. At that time, her "The Death of Society" won the most important British literary award, the Hawthorn Prize. Her works put modern subjective writing into a fairy tale-like atmosphere, so they have a unique flavor. Unfortunately, she later failed to meet everyone's expectations and died unnoticed. The second female novelist is Lady Ball, also a not very famous novelist. In the British translation world,

The Best British Translator

Scott Moncrieff has passed away. He was the translator of two great French writers, MProust and Stendhal. His translations are not only beautiful translations but can even be considered real creations. It is not easy for a translation to be so good. Therefore, the death of Scott Moncrieff is indeed a great loss to the British translation world.

Literary criticism has always been very developed in Britain. There are many kinds of literary criticism publications, including quarterly magazines, monthly magazines, semi-monthly magazines, and weekly magazines, and the most numerous are weekly magazines. The one with the longest history and oldest qualifications among the weekly criticism magazines is "The Saturday Review." However, internal problems have recently occurred in this weekly magazine, involving the authority and personality of the editor, which has become a topic of discussion in the London literary scene for a while. The truth of the matter is this: The chief writer of the Saturday Review was originally Gerald Barry, but Barry was only the chief writer and not the owner of the magazine. In the spring of this year, the owner of the magazine changed his political views and published an article in the weekly magazine without seeking Barry's consent. This method is of course considered acceptable by the owner, but Barry did not change his political views. Therefore, he believed that the owner's actions deprived him of his authority and insulted his personality, so he was furious and protested and resigned immediately. Moreover, not only he himself resigned, but all the special contributors, contributors, and even clerks, typists, and proofreaders resigned together. Moreover, within half a month, a new weekly magazine,

The Week End Review

Not only announced its publication but actually printed it out and sold out completely in a few days. Until now, this weekly magazine is still selling very well. The old contributors to the previous "Saturday Review" are writing articles for it. In addition, famous people such as Shaw and Bennett have joined in to help, so the content is even more exciting and better than the Saturday Review. Barry's independent spirit and perseverance have therefore won a lot of praise. British weekly magazines have always been backed by wealthy politicians, so the opinions of editors and writers are inevitably restricted. The "Saturday Review" incident is an excellent rebellion against this phenomenon, and therefore it has gained the sympathy of many people.

The Poets' Good Fortune

Came with the death of the former Poet Laureate, Dr Beidgss. The attention caused by Bridges' death and the public's speculation about the successor to the Poet Laureate have greatly increased the sales of works by several major British poets. The first to be lucky was naturally John Masefield, the newly appointed Poet Laureate. Because of this sensation, the sales of his poetry collection doubled compared to before. In addition, poets who published new poetry collections during this period were also lucky. Humbert Wolfe is one of them. His new book, "An Uncelestial City," received long and complimentary reviews from various newspapers and magazines, which also brought some fame to the poets. In addition, the South African poet Roy Campbell, although also British, is a new figure in the poetry world, so his poetry collection "Adamarsto" has won a lot of praise.

The Story of World Literature (185)

— Written by John Macy, Translated by Hu Zhongchi

Chapter 48: Essays and History of America

His style, though adorned with various redundancies of rhetoric, is firm and pure. According to the testimony of his contemporaries, Webster was a speaker with powerful voice and dignified attitude, giving a deep impression. Carlyle, who did not have excessive goodwill towards political speakers—or towards Americans—also spoke of Webster's "rock-like strength." He did not always win, because the problems he dealt with were often inherently fragile. However, he has gained a definite place among those who are both world speakers and writers.

Lincoln developed a commendable style from the very beginning of his career. He reached that level through diligent work, not, as the general legend of the Lincoln story says, through the miraculous gift of genius to the ignorant. He was extremely sensitive, extremely wise, cautious, deliberative, and exceptionally endowed with that rare thing misnamed common sense. To this was slightly mixed the illusion of superstition and prophecy. This belongs to the historical politician, not to literature. His style is roughly described as follows:

Please read the Gettysburg Address (Note 1) again, treat it as a short prose poem, a work of art. In a few words, he expresses the emotions of that moment, and he expresses that emotion in a calm and steady style, without embellishment, without high-pitched cries, and with a rhythm carefully planned for the effect he wanted to produce.

Note 1: The speech Lincoln gave at Gettysburg during the Civil War after defeating the Southern Army.

Lincoln's articles are mostly filled with earnest enthusiasm, because he had many difficult problems to solve. However, he also had a lot of humor, which was the salt of his articles and a practical weapon against those who sought office and those who came to harass him. He made them laugh in order to protect himself. When he summoned his cabinet members not to consult them about the Emancipation Proclamation, but to report his decision, he first read several pages of Artemus Ward's (Note 2) works to them. However, after the start of the war, by nature and by circumstances, he was far removed from the agile politician who wanted to tell jokes to the audience in order to win votes. A sad man with a definite purpose and personality, even a politician with policies that we cannot agree with, also learns the use of words. This is one of the lessons learned from the study of expression. Caesar, Cromwell, Napoleon, Bismarck, and Lincoln (remember that I only classify them together from the perspective of studying literature) are masters of a style that is suitable for their work and suitable to the point that it has not yet lost its life. As for criticism, art, and what I think is the extremely bad color of Americanism, I will leave it to prompt the reader to think about it: of all the politicians in the world—please think of Pitt, Disraeli, Gladstone, and whoever from France—Lincoln has the most beautiful and strongest literary color.

Note 2: American humorist, 1834-1867

Art World Guidelines

(1) The text is limited to news, reviews, and introductions of recent art (painting, music, sculpture, architecture, drama, etc.) and literature at home and abroad.

(3) Photos are limited to recent portraits and works of domestic and foreign writers, as well as various photographs related to the text.

Page 19

Book and Newspaper Introduction

Tired Cuckoo's Song, Flying Willow Catkins

— Yang Qiyun

Published by the Founding of the Nation Monthly Magazine

Two days ago, I saw this advertisement in the newspaper: "The first work of the Three Principles of the People literature and art, 'Tired Cuckoo's Song, Flying Willow Catkins,' is published." This stirred me up! But on that day, I was so entangled in my busy work that I couldn't find the time to buy the book and immediately satisfy my desire. That was the reality. I had to endure it, letting my longing grow for a day.

Yesterday, having some free time, I rushed to buy this first work of the Three Principles of the People literature and art. On the way to the bookstore, it seemed as if the streetcar was deliberately trying to make things difficult for me. But no matter how difficult it made things, my desire would eventually be satisfied. Without ceremony, on the way back, I sat on the streetcar and read about a fifth of it in one breath. When I got home, I naturally disregarded all other matters and read it to the end without taking my eyes off it.

To say that "Tired Cuckoo's Song, Flying Willow Catkins" is a creation of Three Principles of the People literature and art, I think it would be more accurate to say that it contains a nationalistic literary color.

"...God, only now have I joined a formal and great battle. I fight for this lovely ancient nation, I fight for this venerable and long history, I fight for this beautiful and magnificent land, and at the same time, I fight to eliminate all feudal remnants."

Isn't this a clear expression of the spirit of striving for the nation? We believe that the war for national survival is necessary and valuable. In the seventh section of the book, this kind of strength, courage, and perseverance are created everywhere, indicating that the future of life is bright. How touching are the words of the character Chu Sheng! He really seems to give people an excitement, allowing them to open their hearts and live bravely, and also enabling them to forget the misfortunes of life, understand the true meaning of life, and even more, enabling the weak in the crossroads to abandon their original decadent thoughts and move towards the positive and bright path of life. Seeing what Chu Sheng and Song Qing said, Song Qing was moved to tears.

Song Qing must decide her own fate. External oppression is not entirely irresistible, and others are powerless to help her decide her fate. Happiness can only be obtained by those who are self-reliant and self-respecting. Song Qing, even if you are in a desperate situation, it is worth it. Even if you die alone, you should die happily. A muddled death is just a special gift from God to the weak. Song Qing, I don't believe you are absolutely hopeless. I believe you have great hope. Song Qing, where has the fire of your life gone? Aren't you looking for it? Song Qing, this is a very easy thing. Quickly find the fire of your life and burn it! Song Qing, how sincerely we expect and hope for it!

People's future is naturally full of infinite hope and endless and great undertakings. Can small setbacks and slight obstacles dominate our great lives? In recent years, the general public has had a considerable awareness of many issues, but naturally, in the old environment, such freedom is not allowed. The latent power in the old environment will naturally come to obstruct everywhere. However, these young people have no way. They only have the ability to realize, but no courage to fight. As a result, they embark on a path of negativity. The so-called youthful era disease is thus accumulated one by one. Song Qing cannot escape this exception. "She is a half-new, half-old character, she knows how to reject shackles, but she doesn't dare to break the famous teachings." She is too tightly forced by Chu Sheng's fierce stimulant. She can only cry. She still has no courage. She is still bound by "old credit and vows." The stubborn old concepts of inheritance do not know how many promising young people have been lost. "What's the use of talking about revolution or no revolution? It's better to solve this problem more practically and concretely." This is indeed the root of our Chinese national character. "To conquer the heart is supreme, to conquer the city is secondary." The Chinese national character transformation movement is the great mission that general literary writers should take on.

Is this a revolutionary literary work? I think everyone must also admit that it is a love work. While advocating conscious ideological reform, it also writes about delicate and pure love everywhere. They are in love with each other, but they do not express it in frivolous actions and language. They only exist in the depths of their hearts, and they both understand that she is willing to present her entire soul to him, and how profound is her affection! Seeing her New Year's greeting letter sent from home, with two red plum blossoms attached, using flowers to speak her mind, how could the recipient forget the beautiful and affectionate writing?

...Chu Sheng, I'm sending you these two plum blossoms, I'm afraid your nose has long forgotten the fragrance of two years ago...Chu Sheng, she is indeed lovely. Her loveliness is not only in the floating fragrance, but in her jade-like heart and bones, in her ice-like integrity...Chu Sheng, please take good care of her. You should look at her often, don't let her feel lonely, but you are not allowed to approach her, otherwise it will make her suffer or even die young...Chu Sheng, stay with her as long as you can. Don't worry in advance that she will wither...Chu Sheng, although she is silent and coldly facing you, she does not reject your love...But Chu Sheng, feel free to love her passionately, just don't forget the one condition that you are not allowed to approach her...

Having received such a deep enjoyment, if it were an average young person, how would they linger and forget his great mission? But the male protagonist in our book does not show it in his actions, neither closely nor distantly. He is not driven by passionate love and intoxicated in the enjoyment of beauty. He still does not forget his own great cause. He gets the opportunity to save the country and the people. He has no hesitation and no fear. He uses swift means to cut through the mess, clearing away obstacles and sweeping away everything. No matter how entangled the environment is, the entangled environment is not enough to stop his great journey. When weighing the pros and cons, he made such a decision: "If it is said that it is good for you personally to love you, it is better to say that as long as I hope you can serve the people and society, it is not a pity to sacrifice yourself. This is what it means to love you."

In short, this book takes into account both revolution and love. While arousing the central consciousness, it also wants to generate the power of life from the writing of love, not to be too intoxicated in the passionate river of love, nor to simply write dry and dull words. In the process of passionate and pure love, it is mixed with powerful consciousness, unconsciously infusing this consciousness into the reader's mind, so that the reader recognizes the great path that life should take. This is where the value of this book lies.

The male protagonist of this book is a promising young man who is rich in emotion, reason, courage, and perseverance. In the decadent and declining Chinese nation, it is really hard to find many. The female protagonist, Song Qing, can be found everywhere in these recent years of the new and old process. In the end, they are all bound by inherited thoughts. "They know how to reject shackles, but they dare not break the famous teachings." They become such sacrifices of the times. In the declining modern Chinese nation, our only hope is that young people like Chu Sheng will continue to increase. We even more hope that there will be people more powerful than Chu Sheng who can work hard to save women like Song Qing who can be awakened but have no courage, break the traditional and inherited ideas, "to conquer the heart is supreme, to conquer the city is secondary." Let us work hard, work hard to transform the national character.

A literary creation with a proper central idea can indeed be regarded as the first collection to discover this "unique banner and brand-new face," and it is naturally worthy of common appreciation. But because I love it so much, I am also critical of it. Please forgive me for contributing some opinions below.

National literature should be written in its own language and script. In this book, the author uses Western letters such as etc. to represent the names of the characters in the book. I think this should be absolutely avoided in national literary works. Moreover, the author uses this kind of pronoun inconsistently before and after. Since Lao Wang is X, Mr. Li is L, and Ziyu is T, then it should be straightforward to write Lao Wang, Mr. Li, and Ziyu. Why bother using X·L·T· to go around in circles in the above paragraphs? If the author thinks this contribution is conscious, then I hope the author will try to change it when it is reprinted.

The Shanghai Tug & Lighter Co., Ltd. at No. 2 Bund, French Concession, declares that the company has been established in Shanghai for many years. It currently has ten tugboats (including four lifeboats, the largest with 1,800 horsepower), three ferries, three harbor tugs, and 115 lighters, each with a load capacity of 50 to 500 tons, with a total load capacity of approximately 20,000 tons. Recently, in order to facilitate combined transportation for customers, 25 cargo trucks have been added, including those that can load large and heavy items up to 20 tons. Recently, major merchants have heard the news and entrusted the company to transport goods due to convenient procedures and fair charges, and business is so brisk that they are overwhelmed.

Theater News

The Changming Film Company declares that the new film "Fire Burning Pingyang City" in two episodes is meticulously produced and even better than the first episode. The first episode focuses on the change of photography, while the second episode retains the strange shooting method while striving for the continuity of the plot. This film has been showing at the Central Theater since the day before yesterday, and the box office is more prosperous than it has been since the theater entered the summer. Anyone who has seen this film cannot help but sigh that it is a rising star in domestic martial arts movies. This film is showing for the last day today at the Central Theater.

The Tongle Amusement Park on Nanjing Road declares that since the opening of the amusement park, it has strived for innovation. Today, the Peking Opera continues to perform two books of "Flying Dragon Biography." The mechanical scenery is quite novel. Every night, there is also a literary tiger waiting for instruction, so literati and elegant guests flock to it. The Baixing Grand Theater declares that since the Heyi Company took over the theater, it has paid more attention to film selection. The theater has already booked the second screening rights in Shanghai for the latest silent blockbusters released by Paramount, United Artists, Fox, and Metro. Therefore, the films shown are all famous. The film "Night Flower" showing today is the largest masterpiece starring the new movie queen, Baraigni Lai. It depicts the prosperity of the dance hall night market, the charming of the dancers, and the methods of seducing men. It is indeed charming and can satisfy the audience.
